<div id="review_2808240900" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2808240900" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2808240900?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2808240900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13173760643078902221"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1557671724ra/27494911.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> Neil had been doing one stupid thing after another all year long and this had turned into the best year of his life.</i><br/><br/>Story 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/>After some time alone or in the company of enemies Neil finally understands that he would do anything for his team - for his chosen family. Anything.<br/>They promised each other to never lose a game ever again - and now they fight with everything they have to hold this promise. <br/>But Neil’s past is more dangerous than anyone of them can imagine and suddenly death threatens the</span>
  <span id="freeText13173760643078902221" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1557671724ra/27494911.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> Neil had been doing one stupid thing after another all year long and this had turned into the best year of his life.</i><br><br>Story 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>After some time alone or in the company of enemies Neil finally understands that he would do anything for his team - for his chosen family. Anything.<br>They promised each other to never lose a game ever again - and now they fight with everything they have to hold this promise. <br>But Neil’s past is more dangerous than anyone of them can imagine and suddenly death threatens the Foxes. <br>If I compare all three books with each other, I’ll probably choose this one as my favorite. <br>It was full of action, friendship, drama, fights and a little bit of something more 😉. <br>I enjoyed it immensely, especially the last 50% or so. I couldn’t stop reading. <br>All in all I’m super happy that I finished this series. It was so much fun and I love my Foxes with my full heart. <br>🦊 <br><br>Character 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>I never had a choice, my heart chose Neil and Andrew as my favorites faster then my mind understood. <br>Their background stories, their personalities, their loyalty and bravery. <br>It was so fascinating and heartbreaking to see that some things they couldn’t quiet understand and sometimes because of their uncertainty they reacted strange and sometimes really bad. <br>While reading this book we really understand this complicated characters and saw how they improved and developed in a positive way. Finally, finally my babies can be happy♥️ <br>By finishing this book I can’t deny my love for the Foxes any longer. Every one of them now has a place in my bookish heart. <br><br>Relationships 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><i> "This," Neil flicked his finger to indicate the two of them, "isn't worthless." <br>"There is no 'this'. This is nothing." <br>"And I am nothing," Neil prompted. When Andrew gestured confirmation, Neil said, "And as you've always said, you want nothing." </i> <br>Oh finally finally my ship has sailed! <br>I’m so happy. <br>Because of his strong run-and-survive-senses Neil never had friends, never really cared enough about anybody and never ever put his life in danger for the safety of others. <br>But when his Foxes and especially Andrew are threatened, Neil sacrifices himself without doubting the decision for one minute. <br>But every time he thinks he will come back and they will throw him out - they show him how much they care about him, how much they love him and want to protect him. <br>And I think Neil needed some times to realize that, but when he did he started to form the Foxes into a real team. <br>And I loved it so much. <br>Finally Neil had a family that loved and cared for him and finally he opened up about everything. <br><br>Writing style 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>Well, even though I loved this book more than the others - I was still a bit bored ca. 7-10% of it and thought about dnf‘ing the book. <br>But only a little bit. I doubted that something interesting would happen but then the book was like „hold my beer 🍺“ and there was so much going on and I couldn’t stop reading because I was so hooked. <br>So, as a new member of the Foxes fandom - read till the end because you’ll love it. <br><br><i> He'd come to the Foxhole Court every inch a lie, but his friends made him into someone real.</i><br><br>P.S. I’m kind of sad that it’s over? Is it too early to reread this book? Hm 🤔<br><br>Reread 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>Still love this book so much. I would reread it again and again till the end of time. <br>Andrew and Neil are the best thing ever ♥️</span>
  <a data-text-id="13173760643078902221" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

  <span id="freeText886819011002713229" style="display:none">OMFG, this was so bloody good!!!<br /><br />No series has ever had such a satisfying ending. The plot kept getting complex with each book and the character development was amazing. I'm in loveeee with Neil, even if baby boy has the survival instincts of a dodo. Even after all the violence, abuse, kidnap and torture, this guy DOES NOT know when to shut up. Good thing he had Andrew to watch his back. These two were adorable! *as adorable as a maniac with a blade can be* <br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed reading about all the other Foxes as well. Coach Wymack is the nicest grouchy character I've ever seen. Wonder of wonders, I even liked Kevin's stuffiness. <br /><br />I loved the team's camaraderie and spirit, their shared love for the sport, their unwavering faith in Neil even after his nth fuck up, the stupidest of bets they had going and the occasional dark humor. And the mafia background was ingenious. Every single thing about this book was crafted to perfection. This book was, in short, unputdownable.</span>

<div id="review_1197304162" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1197304162" />
    <a title="Ais" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8581195-ais"><img alt="Ais" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373253857p2/8581195.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1197304162?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ais" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ais" href="/user/show/8581195-ais">Ais</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=really-good">really-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=glbt">glbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=slash">slash</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8581195-ais?shelf=mysteries-and-death">mysteries-and-death</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1197304162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10535540949988733835">There are no spoilers in this review, for anyone wondering.<br/><br/>--<br/>I just spent all of Sunday rereading the first two books in the series so I could read the third, that I only recently realized had come out. I always get a little worried going into the end of a series, because sometimes the whole previous story gets ruined by choices made in the last book or episode or movie or whatever.<br/><br/>Well. Not the case here. I don't even know why I worried. <br/><br/>The second book left off on a really intense point, and t</span>
  <span id="freeText10535540949988733835" style="display:none">There are no spoilers in this review, for anyone wondering.<br /><br />--<br />I just spent all of Sunday rereading the first two books in the series so I could read the third, that I only recently realized had come out. I always get a little worried going into the end of a series, because sometimes the whole previous story gets ruined by choices made in the last book or episode or movie or whatever.<br /><br />Well. Not the case here. I don't even know why I worried. <br /><br />The second book left off on a really intense point, and the third book started off seamlessly. I tried to write a short review and couldn't because here's the thing: this series is fucking awesome. Any time someone asks me for a m/m series recommendation I ALWAYS recommend this (and Raised by Wolves by WA Hoffman) because this legit is in my top three favorite GLBT series. (RbW and Captive Prince being the others) One of the reasons I love those three series, and especially this series, is because they all have one thing in common: they are stories about things I normally don't like or wouldn't choose to read about, and they are told in such a way where I love the everloving hell out of them.<br /><br />In this series' case: sports. Thing is, I actually really hate sports. There's an active dislike going on with sports, for me. I would rather do almost anything in the world than have to watch a sports game for even an hour. Just, horrendously boring to me. And yet I devoured this three-book series that has a central theme of sports because 1) Exy is pretty cool--I doubt I'd watch any games if it were real life but it's also a game I'd be more likely to think is mildly interesting, and mostly 2) goddamn these characters. <br /><br />I can't really explain to you right now my love for this series. I love that the main characters are seriously messed up individuals and that this is a theme throughout the series. I love that there wasn't some lame thing at the end to force the very destructive and twisted characters to suddenly be "normal" as some sort of superficial happy ending. <br /><br />I actually thought several times throughout the third book how good the editing was (so props to the betas by the way!) because there were very, very few mistakes I found in the text. There were two or three places where, in all honesty, I wish it had been written a little differently: namely, it skimmed a bunch of stuff that I would have liked to have actually seen snippets of dialogue and interaction from, or even better, have the whole thing written out. And a few things that felt like they came a little too easily for everything that had come before to get to that point.<br /><br />But notice how I put 5 stars on this? Yeah. I'm not docking this thing even an iota of a star because it deserves all 5 stars and more. This book had some just, freaking awesome scenes. One in particular I was reading like HOLY SHIT HOLY SHIT NO WHAT IS GOING TO HAPPEN THIS CAN'T HAPPEN RIGHT? and then I looked down at the page count and was like WTF HOW IS THIS ONLY HALFWAY THROUGH THE BOOK?! <br /><br />Also, there are some parts that made me laugh out loud (because of perfectly timed sarcasm or a particularly twisted response to something). I noted several of them because they were great XD Maybe sometime I'll amend this to add them in but I don't have my nook readily available right now.<br /><br />I can tell you one thing, though. This would make a great movie series. And yes, I would watch three movies about this even though sports. Dude, I would watch a whole TV show about this.<br /><br />Let me end on this: I really love the characters but especially Neil and Andrew. The issues they have are so perfectly understandable for them and their lives that it's fantastic and yet they also--I mean, I know I said it before, but seriously. Twisted. But not in a bad way, not in a way where it's making a judgment call about who they are as individuals. I just mean like, definitely not the norm. Andrew has some very extreme reactions to things, and Neil's moral compass is not aligned with most people's. I mean, Andrew physically threatens even his own family members and holds them at knife point, and Neil barely even acknowledges murders and blood and violence but instead focuses on other things. But they also aren't soulless, any of them. Like, despite Neil's high tolerance for violence and seriously skewed moral compass, when he first sees Andrew threaten a family member into silence like described above, he breaks it up and when Andrew leaves he says to the family member, "That is not okay. Don't let him get away with that."<br /><br />Things like that are what I love so much about this whole series, and what continued into this last book. Everyone has facets. And there's a progression of the characters and relationships. Neil definitely grows as a person, Andrew does, everyone does. But Neil especially, you can see the subtle way it happens in places where he doesn't realize his own value.<br /><br />I also like that the book for the most part just goes hardcore into whatever it is it's addressing.<br /><br />Oh, and the relationship--the way it was done was perfect. Nothing was forced in that didn't need to be there, but enough was put in that as a reader I knew exactly what was happening and when and how. Really, really well done on that, because that can be a delicate balance.<br /><br />Nora: please charge more for your work, seriously. I want to give you more money for this. It's unconscionable!<br /><br />Anyway, I will continue to recommend this series any time I'm asked. In all honesty, I do think this series is #1 in my three favorite m/m series list.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10535540949988733835" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2243433206" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3746474545200205717"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I didn't say anything then because I knew I'd look out for only me when the world went to hell. I don't want to be that person anymore. <br/>I want to go back for you." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515421165i/24858716._SY540_.jpg' width='455' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>GUYS.<br/><br/>GUYZZZZZ.<br/><br/>There's this, like, weird ache happening in my chest? And my eyes are like.... dripping and wet? AND HELP SOMEONE HELP I HAVE SO MANY FEELINGGGGSSS!! <br/><br/>NORA SAKAVIC WHAT HAVE YOU DONE TO ME, YOU MONSTER?!<br/><br/>I just sent my brain to her room for not making me read this sooner. <br/><br/>I know I didn't seem too ecstatic in </span>
  <span id="freeText3746474545200205717" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I didn't say anything then because I knew I'd look out for only me when the world went to hell. I don't want to be that person anymore. <br>I want to go back for you." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515421165i/24858716._SY540_.jpg" width="455" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>GUYS.<br><br>GUYZZZZZ.<br><br>There's this, like, weird ache happening in my chest? And my eyes are like.... dripping and wet? AND HELP SOMEONE HELP I HAVE SO MANY FEELINGGGGSSS!! <br><br>NORA SAKAVIC WHAT HAVE YOU DONE TO ME, YOU MONSTER?!<br><br>I just sent my brain to her room for not making me read this sooner. <br><br>I know I didn't seem too ecstatic in my review for book 1, but HOLY HELL if I knew what was to come, I'd gladly rewind and pick this up the SECOND I heard about this series. It took until the end of book 2 for me to understand what the hype was all about, but the build up to all that happens in The King's Men IS. SO. WORTH. IT. The feelings this book pulled from me..wow. I haven't felt this obsessed with characters since I've read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1546272621?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">The Raven Cycle.</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This," Neil flicked his finger to indicate the two of them, "isn't worthless."<br>"There is no 'this'. This is nothing."<br>"And I am nothing," Neil prompted. When Andrew gestured confirmation, Neil said, "And as you've always said, you want nothing."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515421226i/24858718._SY540_.jpg" width="455" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know the blurb makes this sort of sound like a sports YA novel, but don't be fooled. IT IS NOT. It is so so soooo much more.<br><br><i>In summary the All For The Game Series is about:</i><br><br>A group of college students who have been dealt the absolute shittiest cards in life, who have been put together to play a sport that serves as an escape for some but a prison for others, who don't know how or care to get along, but decide to fight and band together and learn that family isn't always what you're born into, but can be who you choose. It's about recovery, and struggles, and not forgetting your past but learning to deal with it and finding out that sometimes, leaning on the ones around you can make it just a little bit easier to get through the day and sometimes, love comes unexpectedly. <br><br>But mostly, it's about a lost boy named Neil who only knows how to run, but finds people who give him so many reasons to stay. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I've never belonged anywhere or had the right to call anything my own. But Coach gave me keys to the court, and you told me to stay. You gave me a key and called it home."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It was sexy and surprisingly romantic and scary and brutal and funny and touching and not at all what I expected and just..just..EVERYTHING. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Yes or no?" <br>"It's always yes with you," Neil said. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/20zq7YP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515421538ra/24858740.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://imgur.com/vMiHZ01" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515421538ra/24858741.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>#ADREILFORFUCKINGLIFE</i>
</b><br><br>The Foxhole Court (All for the Game Book 1) CURRENTLY FREE! | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2m5ya6v">http://amzn.to/2m5ya6v</a><br>The Raven King (All for the Game Book 2) | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2m3VukY">http://amzn.to/2m3VukY</a><br>The King's Men (All for the Game Book 3) | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2F7dljV">http://amzn.to/2F7dljV</a><br><br><i>*credit to gifs <a href="http://aelin.tumblr.com/post/164041782209/if-you-have-to-keep-asking-becauseill-answer-it" rel="nofollow noopener">here.</a></i><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_2276145395" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2276145395" />
    <a title="elias veturius lovebot" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59082429-elias-veturius-lovebot"><img alt="elias veturius lovebot" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600302896p2/59082429.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2276145395?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="elias veturius lovebot" class="user" itemprop="url" name="elias veturius lovebot" href="/user/show/59082429-elias-veturius-lovebot">elias veturius lovebot</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781517198008" href="/book/show/29810309-the-king-s-men">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59082429-elias-veturius-lovebot?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2276145395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13286061322624215538"><b>5/5 Stars</b><br/><br/>This series destroyed me in the best way possible.<br/><br/>I just love these characters so much and their character development. I could read hundreds of pages of them doing literally nothing. I just found Nora Sakavic's Tumblr with all the answers I needed. I can die in peace now. <br/><br/>FINALLY THE ROMANCE I WAS WAITING FOR! And it was so worth the wait, it was just beautiful.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I just adored Neil and Andrew relationship (if you would call that?) it was so much more than just romantic att</span></span>
  <span id="freeText13286061322624215538" style="display:none"><b>5/5 Stars</b><br /><br />This series destroyed me in the best way possible.<br /><br />I just love these characters so much and their character development. I could read hundreds of pages of them doing literally nothing. I just found Nora Sakavic's Tumblr with all the answers I needed. I can die in peace now. <br /><br />FINALLY THE ROMANCE I WAS WAITING FOR! And it was so worth the wait, it was just beautiful.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I just adored Neil and Andrew relationship (if you would call that?) it was so much more than just romantic attraction, it was based on trust and honesty which is as important. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />And the ending was perfect! <br /><br /><b>Trigger Warning:</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This book has torture and mentions sexual abuse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I just found it difficult to read, my heart ached. <br /><br />Neil Josten deserves all the happiness in the world. Words can't describe the amount of love I have for him. And yes, Neil Josten has taken the tile of being my favourite male character of all time. <br /><br />Will I be reading this again in the near future? A hundred times yes!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13286061322624215538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FqD0ThC0vrh9Bh4RWlP+XKqoUypz97FWZZAoWlL/M5mXcytBoxMypD0HMFvidYfTs0dOkfgOcaFsgZghNkTYJg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hOhVXEvf1yAvbztXPCZnwkd65YII59IbkA6wycTWdmUFO4pT+HhbPG9uFR2EAB5NXpX4OYMeEuyZHwCyoG2d2g==')})
  }
